50→\n    51→class RateLimitMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):\n    52→    def __init__(self, app):\n    53→        super().__init__(app)\n    54→        self._fallback_counters: dict[str, list[float]] = defaultdict(list)\n    55→\n    56→    async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next):\n    57→        client_ip = request.client.host if request.client else \"unknown\"\n    58→        path = request.url.path\n    59→\n    60→        # Find applicable rate limit\n    61→        limit, window = DEFAULT_LIMIT\n    62→        for prefix, (lim, win) in RATE_LIMITS.items():\n    63→ > 4 else 'default'}\"\n    68→\n    69→        # Try Redis first (shared across all workers)\n    70→        r = _get_redis()\n    71→        if r:\n    72→            try:\n    73→      if count >= limit:\n    83→                    return JSONResponse(\n    84→                        status_code=429,\n    85→                        content={\"detail\": \"Rate limit exceeded\", \"retry_after\": window},\n    86→                        headers={\"Retry-After\": str(window)},\n    87→                    )\n    88→\n    89→                return await call_next(request)\n    90→            except Exception:\n    91→                pass  # Fall through to in-memory\n    92→\n    93→        # Fallback: in-memory per-worker counter\n    94→        now = time.time()\n    95→        self._fallback_counters[key] = [\n    96→            t for t in self._fallback_counters[key] if t > now - window\n    97→        ]\n    98→\n    99→        if len(self._fallback_counters[key]) \"disconnected\" | \"error\";\n     8→\n     9→interface UseWebSocketOptions {\n    10→  /** WebSocket channel path, e.g. \"/ws/incidents\" */\n    11→  channel: string;\n    12→  /** Called when a message is received */\n    13→  onMessage?: (msg: WSMessage) => void;\n    14→  /** Auto-connect on mount (default: true) */\n    15→  autoConnect?: boolean;\n    16→}\n    17→\n    18→/**\n    19→ * WebSocket hook with JWT auth, exponential backoff reconnect,\n    20→ * and app state awareness (pauses when backgrounded).\n    21→ */\n    22→export function useWebSocket({ channel, onMessage, autoConnect = true }: UseWebSocketOptions) {\n    23→  const [state, setState] = useState<ConnectionState>(\"disconnected\");\n    24→  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null);\n    25→  const reconnectTimer = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);\n    26→  const reconnectAttempts = useRef(0);\n    27→  const onMessageRef = useRef(onMessage);\n    28→  const isMounted = useRef(true);\n    29→\n    30→  // Keep onMessage ref current without re-triggering effects\n    31→  useEffect(() => {\n    32→    onMessageRef.current = onMessage;\n    33→  }, [onMessage]);\n    34→\n    35→  const getBackendWsUrl = useCallback(async (): Promise<string | null> => {\n    36→    const token = await getAccessToken();\n    37→    if (!token) return null;\n    38→\n    39→    const httpUrl = process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_BACKEND_URL;\n    40→    if (!httpUrl) return null;\n    41→\n    42→    const wsUrl = httpUrl.replace(/^http/, \"ws\");\n    43→    return `${wsUrl}/api/v1${channel}?token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}`;\n    44→  }, [channel]);\n    45→\n    46→  const connect = useCallback(async () => {\n    47→    if (wsRef.current?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) return;\n    48→\n    49→    const url = await getBackendWsUrl();\n    50→    if (!url || !isMounted.current) return;\n    51→\n    52→    setState(\"connecting\");\n    53→    const ws = new WebSocket(url);\n    54→\n    55→    ws.onopen = () => {\n    56→      if (!isMounted.current) return;\n    57→      setState(\"connected\");\n    58→      reconnectAttempts.current = 0;\n    59→    };\n    60→\n    61→    ws.onmessage = (event) => {\n    62→      try {\n    63→        const msg: WSMessage = JSON.parse(event.data);\n    64→        onMessageRef.current?.(msg);\n    65→      } catch {\n    66→        // Ignore unparseable messages\n    67→      }\n    68→    };\n    69→\n    70→    ws.onclose = (event) => {\n    71→      if (!isMounted.current) return;\n    72→      setState(\"disconnected\");\n    73→\n    74→      // Auth errors: don't reconnect (user needs to re-login)\n    75→      if (event.code === 4001 || event.code === 4003) {\n    76→        return;\n    77→      }\n    78→\n    79→      // Schedule reconnect with exponential backoff\n    80→      const delay = Math.min(\n    81→        WS.RECONNECT_BASE_MS * Math.pow(2, reconnectAttempts.current),\n    82→        WS.RECONNECT_MAX_MS\n    83→      );\n    84→      reconnectAttempts.current += 1;\n    85→      reconnectTimer.current = setTimeout(() => {\n    86→        if (isMounted.current) connect();\n    87→      }, delay);\n    88→    };\n    89→\n    90→    ws.onerror = () => {\n    91→      if (!isMounted.current) return;\n    92→      setState(\"error\");\n    93→    };\n    94→\n    95→    wsRef.current = ws;\n    96→  }, [getBackendWsUrl]);\n    97→\n    98→  const disconnect = useCallback(() => {\n    99→    if (reconnectTimer.current) {\n   100→      clearTimeout(reconnectTimer.current);\n   101→      reconnectTimer.current = null;\n   102→    }\n   103→    if (wsRef.current) {\n   104→      wsRef.current.close();\n   105→      wsRef.current = null;\n   106→    }\n   107→    setState(\"disconnected\");\n   108→  }, []);\n   109→\n   110→  // Auto-connect on mount\n   111→  useEffect(() => {\n   112→    isMounted.current = true;\n   113→    if (autoConnect) connect();\n   114→\n   115→    return () => {\n   116→      isMounted.current = false;\n   117→      disconnect();\n   118→    };\n   119→  }, [autoConnect, connect, disconnect]);\n   120→\n   121→  // Pause/resume on app state changes\n   122→  useEffect(() => {\n   123→    const handleAppState = (nextState: AppStateStatus) => {\n   124→      if (nextState === \"active\" && state === \"disconnected\") {\n   125→        reconnectAttempts.current = 0;\n   126→        connect();\n   127→      } else if (nextState === \"background\") {\n   128→        disconnect();\n   129→ 136→  return { state, connect, disconnect };\n   137→}\n - `notification_worker.py` -- `send_email_notification` (SMTP), `send_webhook_notification` (HTTP POST + HMAC), `send_sms_notification` (Twilio), `send_push_notification` (FCM); all with circuit `flooreye`\n\n**Redis (`redis`)**\n- **What**: Cache, message broker, rate limiter, WebSocket PubSub -- Redis 7.2 Alpine\n- **Port**: 6379\n- **Connects TO**: Nothing (passive)\n- **Connected TO BY**: Backend (DB0: cache + PubSub + rate limiting), Worker (DB1: Celery broker, DB2: Celery results)\n- **Protocol**: RESP (Redis Protocol over TCP)\n\n**MinIO (`minio`)** (production only)\n- **What**: tunnel, browsers\n- **Protocol**: HTTP/1.1 (proxies both REST and WebSocket with upgrade headers)\n- **Routes**: `/api/*` -> backend, `/ws/*` -> backend (upgrade), `/*` -> SPA static to local services\n\n### 1.2 Edge Agent Stack (On-Premise, per-Store)\n\n**Edge Agent (`edge-agent`)**\n- **What**: Frame capture, inference orchestration, upload, device control -- Python async\n- auto-clip recording\n\n**Inference Server (`inference-server`)**\n- **What**: ONNX Runtime model serving -- FastAPI\n- **Port**: 8080 (bound to 127.0.0.1 only)\n- **Connects TO**: Nothing (reads /models volume)\n- **Connected TO BY**: Edge Agent (HTTP)\n- **Protocol**: HTTP/1.1 REST\n- **Endpoints**: `/health`, `/infer`, `/infer-batch`, `/load-model`, `/model/download`, `/model/info`\n- **GPU**: NVIDIA GPU reservation (nvidia driver, 1 GPU)\n\n**Redis Buffer (`redis-buffer`)**\n- **What**: Frame queue + offline buffer -- Redis 7 Alpine with AOF persistence\n- **Port**: 6379 (internal policy\n\n**Cloudflared (Edge)** (`cloudflared`)\n- **What**: Secure tunnel from edge to cloud\n- **Port**: None exposed\n- **Connects TO**: Cloudflare edge network (HTTPS outbound)\n- **Connected TO DATA FLOW SUMMARY\n\n### Detection Flow (Edge-First)\n```\nCamera --RTSP--> Edge Agent --HTTP--> Inference Server (ONNX)\n                     |\n                     v\n              4-Layer Validation (local)\n                     |\n                     v\n              Redis Buffer (offline queue)\n                     |\n                     v\n              Uploader --HTTPS--> Cloud Backend --TCP--> MongoDB\n                                       |\n                                       v\n                                  Redis PubSub --WS--> Web/Mobile clients\n                                       |\n                                       v\n                                  Celery Worker --> Notifications\n                                       |\n                                  SMTP / FCM / Twilio / Webhook\n```\n\n### Command Flow (Cloud to Edge)\n```\nWeb UI --> Backend API --> MongoDB (edge_commands)\n                              |\nEdge Agent (polls /30s) <-----+\n     |\n     v\nExecute: deploy_model, reload_config, restart_camera, etc.\n```\n\n## 4. PORT MAP\n\n| Service | Port | Protocol | Binding |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| FastAPI Backend | 8000 | HTTP/WS | 0.0.0.0 |\n| MongoDB | 27017 | TCP (Wire) | 0.0.0.0 (dev), internal (prod) |\n| Redis (Cloud) | 6379 | TCP (RESP) | 0.0.0.0 (dev), internal (prod) |\n| MinIO API | 9000 | HTTP (S3) | internal |\n| MinIO Console | 9001 | HTTP | internal |\n| Nginx | 80 | HTTP | 0.0.0.0 |\n| Edge Inference Server | 8080 | HTTP | 127.0.0.1 only |\n| Edge Agent Web UI | 8090 | HTTP | 0.0.0.0 |\n| Edge Agent Config API | 8091 | HTTP | 0.0.0.0 |\n| Edge Redis Buffer | 6379 | TCP (RESP) | internal |\n| Web Dev Server (Vite) | 5173 | HTTP | dev only |\n\n## 5. KEY ARCHITECTURAL DECISIONS\n\n1. **Edge-first inference**: YOLO26 ONNX runs locally on edge GPU; cloud Roboflow is fallback only.\n2. **Redis triple-duty**: Cache/PubSub (DB0), Celery broker (DB1), Celery results (DB2) -- single Redis instance in cloud.\n3. **Separate edge Redis**: Independent Redis on edge for frame buffering with LRU eviction, survives cloud disconnection.\n4. **Cloudflare Tunnel both sides**: Cloud side tunnels public traffic in; edge side tunnels to Cloudflare for secure egress without open ports.\n5. **Polling not push for commands**: Edge agent polls backend every 30s for commands (no inbound ports needed).\n6. **Circuit breaker pattern**: All notification channels (SMTP, FCM, Twilio, webhook) have independent circuit breakers.\n7. **WebSocket via Redis PubSub**: Broadcasts work across multiple Gunicorn workers via PSUBSCRIBE on `ws:*` pattern."}],"stop_reason":"end_turn","stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1729,"cache_read_input_tokens":75538,"output_tokens":7236,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1729},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"}},"requestId":"req_011CZJQf9245Wby1LbkMTKAk","type":"assistant","uuid":"51a5cf7b-4b34-4e58-b3ca-09d89158965d","timestamp":"2026-03-22T16:11:17.057Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"C:\\Users\\jshah\\flooreye","sessionId":"31c38874-0fdd-46a7-87a9-fa414d8b993d","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"warm-exploring-rossum"}
